- Tingling in Hands and Feet


# History of Present Illness
Lenny728
 is a 75 year-old nonhispanic white male. Patient has a history of gingival disease (disorder), end-stage renal disease (disorder), chronic kidney disease stage 3 (disorder), concussion with no loss of consciousness (disorder), medication review due (situation), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), chronic kidney disease stage 4 (disorder), part-time employment (finding), acute bronchitis (disorder), concussion injury of brain (disorder), chronic kidney disease stage 2 (disorder), limited social contact (finding), not in labor force (finding), chronic kidney disease stage 1 (disorder), primary dental caries (disorder), infection of tooth (disorder), full-time employment (finding), awaiting transplantation of kidney (situation), dental filling lost (finding), gingivitis (disorder), myocardial infarction (disorder), social isolation (finding), stress (finding).

# Social History
Patient is single. Patient quit smoking at age 16.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has completed some college courses.
Patient currently has Medicare.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
lisinopril 10 mg oral tablet; 1 ml epoetin alfa 4000 unt/ml injection [epogen]; acetaminophen 325 mg oral tablet; heparin sodium, porcine 100 unt/ml injectable solution; hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; 1 ml tacrolimus 5 mg/ml injection; amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet; insulin lispro 100 unt/ml injectable solution [humalog]; aspirin 325 mg oral tablet; clopidogrel 300 mg oral tablet; 24 hr tacrolimus 1 mg extended release oral tablet; sodium fluoride 0.0272 mg/mg oral gel

- Tingling in Hands and Feet


# History of Present Illness
Lenny728
 is a 68 year-old nonhispanic white male. Patient has a history of gingival disease (disorder), chronic kidney disease stage 3 (disorder), concussion with no loss of consciousness (disorder), medication review due (situation), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), chronic kidney disease stage 4 (disorder), part-time employment (finding), concussion injury of brain (disorder), chronic kidney disease stage 2 (disorder), limited social contact (finding), not in labor force (finding), chronic kidney disease stage 1 (disorder), infection of tooth (disorder), full-time employment (finding), awaiting transplantation of kidney (situation), dental filling lost (finding), gingivitis (disorder), social isolation (finding), stress (finding).

# Social History
Patient is single. Patient quit smoking at age 16.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has completed some college courses.
Patient currently has Medicare.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
lisinopril 10 mg oral tablet; 1 ml epoetin alfa 4000 unt/ml injection [epogen]; hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet; insulin lispro 100 unt/ml injectable solution [humalog]; sodium fluoride 0.0272 mg/mg oral gel

# Assessment and Plan


## Plan

The following procedures were conducted:
- renal dialysis (procedure)
The patient was prescribed the following medications:
- 1 ml epoetin alfa 4000 unt/ml injection [epogen]

# History of Present Illness
Lenny728
 is a 67 year-old nonhispanic white male. Patient has a history of gingival disease (disorder), chronic kidney disease stage 3 (disorder), concussion with no loss of consciousness (disorder), medication review due (situation), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), chronic kidney disease stage 4 (disorder), part-time employment (finding), concussion injury of brain (disorder), chronic kidney disease stage 2 (disorder), limited social contact (finding), not in labor force (finding), chronic kidney disease stage 1 (disorder), infection of tooth (disorder), full-time employment (finding), awaiting transplantation of kidney (situation), dental filling lost (finding), gingivitis (disorder), social isolation (finding), stress (finding).

# Social History
Patient is single. Patient quit smoking at age 16.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has completed some college courses.
Patient currently has Medicare.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
lisinopril 10 mg oral tablet; 1 ml epoetin alfa 4000 unt/ml injection [epogen]; hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet; insulin lispro 100 unt/ml injectable solution [humalog]; sodium fluoride 0.0272 mg/mg oral gel

# Assessment and Plan


## Plan

The following procedures were conducted:
- renal dialysis (procedure)
The patient was prescribed the following medications:
- 1 ml epoetin alfa 4000 unt/ml injection [epogen]
